103:["$","annotation",null,{"encoding":"application/x-tex","children":"\\begin{aligned}\nH(M) &= I(M; S_\\mathcal{T}) + H(M|S_\\mathcal{T}) \\text{(by def. of mutual information)}\\\\\n&= I(M; S_\\mathcal{T}) \\text{(since }S_\\mathcal{T}\\text{ suffice to decode M)}\\\\\n&= I(M; S_{i_t}, S_\\mathcal{Z}) \\text{(since }S_\\mathcal{T} = S_\\mathcal{Z} ∪ S_{i_t})\\\\\n&= I(M; S_{i_t}|S_\\mathcal{Z}) + I(M; S_\\mathcal{Z}) \\text{(chain rule)}\\\\\n&= I(M; S_{i_t}|S_\\mathcal{Z}) \\text{(since }\\mathcal{Z}\\leq z \\text{, it reveals nothing about M)}\\\\\n&= I(S_{i_t}; M|S_\\mathcal{Z}) \\text{(symmetry of mutual information)}\\\\\n&= H(S_{i_t}|S_\\mathcal{Z}) - H(S_{i_t}|M,S_\\mathcal{Z}) \\text{(def. of conditional mutual information)}\\\\\n&\\leq H(S_{i_t}|S_\\mathcal{Z}) \\text{(entropy is non-negative)}\\\\\n&\\leq H(S_{i_t}|S_\\mathcal{Z}) \\text{(conditioning reduces entropy)} \\\\\n\\end{aligned}"}]
